<span data-ttu-id="49104-332">Il testo letterale diverso dai parametri di route, ad esempio `{id}`, e il separatore di percorso `/` devono corrispondere al testo nell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-332">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-333">La corrispondenza del testo non fa distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole e si basa sulla rappresentazione decodificata del percorso degli URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-333">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-334">Per verificare la corrispondenza di un delimitatore letterale dei parametri di route (`{` o `}`), eseguire l'escape del delimitatore ripetendo il carattere (`{{` o `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-334">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-335">I modelli di URL che tentano di acquisire un nome file con un'estensione facoltativa hanno considerazioni aggiuntive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-335">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-336">Considerare ad esempio il modello `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-336">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-337">Se esistono i valori per `filename` e `ext`, vengono popolati entrambi i valori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-337">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-338">Se esiste solo un valore per `filename` nell'URL, la route corrisponde perché il punto finale (`.`) è facoltativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-338">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-339">Gli URL seguenti corrispondono a questa route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-339">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="49104-340">È possibile usare un asterisco (`*`) o un doppio asterisco (`**`) come prefisso per un parametro di route da associare alla parte rimanente dell'URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-340">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-341">Si tratta di parametri chiamati parametri *catch-all*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-341">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-342">Ad esempio, `blog/{**slug}` corrisponde a qualsiasi URI che inizia con `/blog` seguito da qualsiasi valore, che viene assegnato al valore di route `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-342">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-343">I parametri catch-all possono anche corrispondere alla stringa vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-343">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-344">Il parametro catch-all esegue l'escape dei caratteri appropriati, incluso il separatore di percorso (`/`), quando la route viene usata per generare un URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-344">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-345">Ad esempio, la route `foo/{*path}` con i valori di route `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-345">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-346">Si noti la barra di escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-346">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-347">Per eseguire il round trip dei caratteri di separatore di percorso, usare il prefisso del parametro di route `**`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-347">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-348">La route `foo/{**path}` con `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my/path`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-348">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-349">I parametri di route possono avere *valori predefiniti*, definiti specificando il valore predefinito dopo il nome del parametro, separato da un segno di uguale (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-349">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-350">Ad esempio, `{controller=Home}` definisce `Home` come valore predefinito per `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-350">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-351">Il valore predefinito viene usato se nell'URL non è presente alcun valore per il parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-351">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-352">I parametri di route vengono resi facoltativi aggiungendo un punto interrogativo (`?`) alla fine del nome del parametro, come in `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-352">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-353">La differenza tra parametri facoltativi e parametri di route predefiniti è che un parametro di route con un valore predefinito produce sempre un valore, mentre un parametro facoltativo ha un valore solo se ne viene specificato uno dall'URL della richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-353">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-354">I parametri di route possono presentare dei vincoli che devono corrispondere al valore di route associato dall'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-354">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-355">Aggiungendo due punti (`:`) e il nome del vincolo dopo il nome del parametro di route, si specifica un *vincolo inline* per un parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-355">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-356">Se il vincolo richiede argomenti, vengono racchiusi tra parentesi (`(...)`) dopo il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-356">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-357">È possibile specificare più vincoli inline aggiungendo di nuovo i due punti (`:`) e il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-357">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-358">Il nome del vincolo e gli argomenti vengono passati al servizio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> per creare un'istanza di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> da usare nell'elaborazione dell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-358">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-359">Il modello di route `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifica ad esempio un vincolo `minlength` con l'argomento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-359">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-360">Per altre informazioni sui vincoli di route e per un elenco dei vincoli specificati dal framework, vedere la sezione [Riferimento per i vincoli di route](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-360">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-361">I parametri di route possono avere anche trasformatori di parametro che trasformano un valore di parametro durante la generazione dei collegamenti e l'abbinamento delle azioni e delle pagine agli URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-361">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-362">Come i vincoli, i trasformatori di parametro possono essere aggiunti inline a un parametro di route inserendo due punti (`:`) e il nome del trasformatore dopo il nome del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-362">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-363">Ad esempio, il modello di route `blog/{article:slugify}` specifica un trasformatore `slugify`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-363">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-364">Per altre informazioni sui trasformatori di parametro, vedere la sezione [Riferimento ai trasformatori di parametro](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-364">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-365">La tabella seguente illustra i modelli di route di esempio e il relativo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-365">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-366">Modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-366">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="49104-367">URI corrispondente di esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-367">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-368">L'URI della richiesta&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-368">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="49104-369">Verifica la corrispondenza solo del singolo percorso `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-369">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-370">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-370">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="49104-371">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-371">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="49104-372">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e all'azione `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-372">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-373">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e all'azione `Details` (`id` impostato su 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-373">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-374">Esegue il mapping al controller `Home` e al metodo `Index` (`id` viene ignorato).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-374">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-375">L'uso di un modello è in genere l'approccio più semplice al routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-375">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-376">I vincoli e le impostazioni predefinite possono essere specificati anche all'esterno del modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-376">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-377">Abilitare la [registrazione](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) per verificare in che modo le implementazioni del routing predefinite, ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, corrispondono alle richieste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-377">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-378">Nomi riservati di routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-378">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-379">Le parole chiave seguenti sono nomi riservati e non possono essere usate come nomi o parametri di route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-379">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-380">Riferimento per i vincoli di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-380">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-381">I vincoli di route vengono eseguiti quando si verifica una corrispondenza nell'URL in ingresso e il percorso URL viene suddiviso in valori di route in formato token.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-381">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-382">I vincoli di route in genere controllano il valore di route associato usando il modello di route e stabiliscono con una decisione Sì/No se il valore è accettabile o meno.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-382">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-383">Alcuni vincoli di route usano i dati all'esterno del valore di route per stabilire se la richiesta può essere instradata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-383">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-384">Ad esempio, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> può accettare o rifiutare una richiesta in base al relativo verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-384">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-385">I vincoli vengono usati nelle richieste del routing e nella generazione di collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-385">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-386">Non usare i vincoli per la **convalida dell'input**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-386">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-387">Se vengono usati vincoli per la **convalida dell'input**, un input non valido causa la visualizzazione di un errore di tipo *404 (Non trovato)* invece di un errore di tipo *400 - Richiesta non valida* con un messaggio di errore appropriato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-387">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-388">I vincoli di route vengono usati per evitare **ambiguità** tra route simili, non per convalidare gli input per una route specifica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-388">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-389">La tabella seguente illustra i vincoli di route di esempio e il relativo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-389">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-390">vincolo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-390">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-391">Esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-391">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-392">Esempi di corrispondenza</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-392">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-393">Note</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-393">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-394">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-394">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-395">Corrisponde a qualsiasi numero intero</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-395">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-396">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-396">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-397">Corrisponde a `true` o `false` (senza distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-397">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-398">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-398">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-399">Corrisponde a un valore `DateTime` valido (impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica, vedere avviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-399">Matches a valid `DateTime` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-400">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-400">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-401">Corrisponde a un valore `decimal` valido (impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica, vedere avviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-401">Matches a valid `decimal` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-402">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-402">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-403">Corrisponde a un valore `double` valido (impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica, vedere avviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-403">Matches a valid `double` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-404">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-404">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-405">Corrisponde a un valore `float` valido (impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica, vedere avviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-405">Matches a valid `float` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-406">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-406">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-407">Corrisponde a un valore `Guid` valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-407">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-408">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-408">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-409">Corrisponde a un valore `long` valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-409">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-410">La stringa deve contenere almeno 4 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-410">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-411">La stringa non deve contenere più di 8 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-411">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-412">La stringa deve contenere esattamente 12 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-412">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-413">La stringa deve contenere almeno 8 e non più di 16 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-413">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-414">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-414">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-415">Il valore intero non deve essere superiore a 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-415">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-416">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18 ma non più di 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-416">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-417">La stringa deve essere costituita da uno o più caratteri alfabetici (`a`-`z`, senza distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-417">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-418">La stringa deve corrispondere all'espressione regolare (vedere i suggerimenti per la definizione di un'espressione regolare)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-418">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-419">Usato per imporre che un valore diverso da un parametro sia presente durante la generazione dell'URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-419">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-420">Più vincoli delimitati da punti possono essere applicati a un singolo parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-420">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-421">Ad esempio il vincolo seguente limita un parametro a un valore intero maggiore o uguale a 1:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-421">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-422">I vincoli di route che verificano l'URL e vengono convertiti in un tipo CLR, ad esempio `int` o `DateTime`, usano sempre le impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-422">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-423">presupponendo che l'URL sia non localizzabile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-423">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-424">I vincoli di route specificati dal framework non modificano i valori archiviati nei valori di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-424">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-425">Tutti i valori di route analizzati dall'URL vengono archiviati come stringhe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-425">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-426">Ad esempio, il vincolo `float` prova a convertire il valore di route in un valore float, ma il valore convertito viene usato solo per verificare che può essere convertito in un valore float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-426">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-427">Espressioni regolari</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-427">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-428">Il framework di ASP.NET Core aggiunge `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` al costruttore di espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-428">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-429">Per una descrizione di questi membri, vedere <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-429">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-430">Le espressioni regolari usano delimitatori e token simili a quelli usati dal routing e dal linguaggio C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-430">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-431">Per i token di espressione è necessario aggiungere caratteri di escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-431">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-432">Per usare l'espressione regolare `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` nel routing, l'espressione deve includere i caratteri `\` (barra rovesciata singola) specificati nella stringa come caratteri `\\` (barra rovesciata doppia) nel file di origine C# per eseguire l'escape del carattere di escape della stringa `\`, a meno che non si usino [valori letterali di stringa verbatim](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-432">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-433">Per eseguire l'escape dii caratteri delimitatori dei parametri di routing (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), raddoppiare i caratteri nell'espressione (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-433">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-434">La tabella seguente mostra un'espressione regolare e la versione dopo l'escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-434">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-435">Espressione regolare</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-435">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-436">Espressione regolare con caratteri di escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-436">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-437">Le espressioni regolari usate nel routing spesso iniziano con l'accento circonflesso (`^`) e corrispondono alla posizione iniziale della stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-437">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-438">Le espressioni spesso terminano con il segno di dollaro (`$`) e corrispondono alla fine della stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-438">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-439">I caratteri `^` e `$` consentono di verificare che l'espressione regolare corrisponda all'intero valore del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-439">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-440">Senza i caratteri `^` e `$` l'espressione regolare corrisponde a qualsiasi sottostringa all'interno della stringa e spesso questo non è il risultato desiderato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-440">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-441">La tabella seguente include alcuni esempi e descrive perché si verifica o non si verifica la corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-441">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-442">Expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-442">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-443">Stringa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-443">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-444">Corrispondenza con</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-444">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-445">Commento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-445">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-446">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-446">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-447">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-447">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-448">Corrispondenze di sottostringhe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-448">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-449">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-449">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-450">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-450">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-451">Corrispondenze di sottostringhe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-451">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-452">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-452">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="49104-453">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-453">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-454">Corrisponde all'espressione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-454">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-455">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-455">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="49104-456">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-456">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-457">Senza distinzione maiuscole/minuscole</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-457">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-458">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-458">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-459">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-459">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-460">Vedere `^` e `$` sopra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-460">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-461">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-461">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-462">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-462">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-463">Vedere `^` e `$` sopra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-463">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-464">Per altre informazioni sulla sintassi delle espressioni regolari, vedere [Espressioni regolari di .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-464">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-465">Per limitare un parametro a un set noto di valori possibili, usare un'espressione regolare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-465">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-466">Ad esempio, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` verifica la corrispondenza del valore di route `action` solo con `list`, `get` o `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-466">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-467">Se viene passata nel dizionario di vincoli, la stringa `^(list|get|create)$` è equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-467">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-468">Anche i vincoli passati nel dizionario di vincoli (non inline all'interno di un modello) che non corrispondono a uno dei vincoli noti vengono considerati espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-468">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-469">Vincoli di route personalizzati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-469">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-470">Oltre ai vincoli di route predefiniti, è possibile creare vincoli di route personalizzati implementando l'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-470">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-471">L'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contiene un singolo metodo, `Match`, che restituisce `true` se il vincolo viene soddisfatto e `false` in caso contrario.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-471">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-472">Per usare un'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personalizzata, il tipo di vincolo di route deve essere registrato con la proprietà <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> dell'app nel contenitore di servizi dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-472">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-473"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> è un dizionario che esegue il mapping delle chiavi dei vincoli di route alle implementazioni di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> che convalidano tali vincoli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-473">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-474">La proprietà <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> di un'app può essere aggiornata in `Startup.ConfigureServices` come parte di una chiamata [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) o configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> direttamente con `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-474">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-475">Esempio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-475">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-476">Il vincolo può quindi essere applicato alle route nel modo consueto, usando il nome specificato al momento della registrazione del tipo di vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-476">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-477">Esempio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-477">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-478">Riferimento ai trasformatori di parametro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-478">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-479">I trasformatori di parametro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-479">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="49104-480">Vengono eseguiti quando si genera un collegamento per <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-480">Execute when generating a link for a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-481">Implementare `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-481">Implement `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-482">Vengono configurati tramite <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-482">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-483">Acquisire il valore della route del parametro e trasformarlo in un nuovo valore stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-483">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-484">Il valore trasformato viene usato nel collegamento generato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-484">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-485">Ad esempio, un trasformatore di parametro `slugify` personalizzato nel modello di route `blog\{article:slugify}` con `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` genera `blog\my-test-article`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-485">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-486">Per usare un trasformatore di parametro in un modello di route, configurarlo prima usando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-486">To use a parameter transformer in a route pattern, configure it first using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    // Replace the type and the name used to refer to it with your own
    // IOutboundParameterTransformer implementation
    options.ConstraintMap["slugify"] = typeof(SlugifyParameterTransformer);
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-487">I trasformatori di parametro sono usati dai framework per trasformare l'URI in cui viene risolto un endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-487">Parameter transformers are used by the framework to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-488">Ad esempio, ASP.NET Core MVC usa i trasformatori di parametro per trasformare il valore di route usato per abbinare `area`, `controller`, `action` e `page`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-488">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC uses parameter transformers to transform the route value used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller:slugify=Home}/{action:slugify=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-489">Con la route precedente, l'azione `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` viene abbinata all'URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-489">With the preceding route, the action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` is matched with the URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-490">Un trasformatore di parametro non modifica i valori della route usati per generare un collegamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-490">A parameter transformer doesn't change the route values used to generate a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-491">Ad esempio, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` restituisce `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-491">For example, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` outputs `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-492">ASP.NET Core offre convenzioni API per l'uso di trasformatori di parametro con le route generate:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-492">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using a parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="49104-493">ASP.NET Core MVC include la convenzione API `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-493">ASP.NET Core MVC has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-494">Questa convenzione applica un trasformatore di parametro specifico a tutte le route di attributi nell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-494">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-495">Il trasformatore di parametro trasforma i token di route di attributi man mano che vengono sostituiti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-495">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-496">Per altre informazioni vedere [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement) (Usare un trasformatore di parametro per personalizzare la sostituzione di token).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-496">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-497">Razor Pages include la convenzione API `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-497">Razor Pages has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-498">Questa convenzione applica un trasformatore di parametro specificato a tutte le istanze di Razor Pages individuate automaticamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-498">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-499">Il trasformatore di parametro trasforma la cartella e i segmenti di nome file delle route di Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-499">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-500">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes) (Usare un trasformatore di parametro per personalizzare route di pagine).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-500">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-501">Riferimento per la generazione di URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-501">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-502">L'esempio seguente mostra come generare un collegamento a una route usando un dizionario di valori di route e un elemento <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-502">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="49104-503">L'elemento <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generato alla fine dell'esempio precedente è `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-503">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-504">Il dizionario fornisce i valori di route `operation` e `id` del modello "Track Package Route", `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-504">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-505">Per informazioni dettagliate, vedere il codice di esempio nella sezione [Usare il middleware di routing](#use-routing-middleware) oppure l'[app di esempio](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-505">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-506">Il secondo parametro per il costruttore <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> è una raccolta di *valori di ambiente*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-506">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-507">I valori di ambiente sono utili poiché limitano il numero di valori che uno sviluppatore deve specificare all'interno del contesto di una richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-507">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-508">I valori di route correnti della richiesta corrente sono considerati valori di ambiente per la generazione del collegamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-508">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-509">Nell'azione `About` di un'app ASP.NET Core MVC di `HomeController`, non è necessario specificare il valore di route del controller per collegarsi all'azione `Index`. Viene usato il valore di ambiente `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-509">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-510">I valori di ambiente che non corrispondono a un parametro vengono ignorati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-510">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-511">I valori di ambiente vengono ignorati anche quando un valore specificato in modo esplicito esegue l'override del valore di ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-511">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-512">La corrispondenza si verifica da sinistra a destra nell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-512">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-513">I valori specificati in modo esplicito ma che non corrispondono a un segmento della route vengono aggiunti alla stringa di query.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-513">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-514">La tabella seguente illustra il risultato ottenuto quando si usa il modello di route `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-514">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-515">Valori di ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-515">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-516">Valori espliciti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-516">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="49104-517">Risultato</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-517">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="49104-518">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-518">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="49104-519">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-519">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="49104-520">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-520">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="49104-521">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-521">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="49104-522">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-522">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-523">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-523">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="49104-524">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-524">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="49104-525">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-525">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-526">Se una route ha un valore predefinito che non corrisponde a un parametro e tale valore viene specificato in modo esplicito, deve corrispondere al valore predefinito:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-526">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-527">La generazione dei collegamenti genera un collegamento per questa route quando vengono specificati i valori corrispondenti per `controller` e `action`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-527">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-528">Segmenti complessi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-528">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-529">I segmenti complessi (ad esempio, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`), vengono elaborati individuando corrispondenze per i valori letterali da destra a sinistra in modalità non-greedy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-529">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-530">Vedere [questo codice](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) per una spiegazione dettagliata di come vengono confrontati i segmenti complessi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-530">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-531">L'[esempio di codice](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) non viene usato da ASP.NET Core, ma offre una spiegazione esauriente dei segmenti complessi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-531">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>

The [current code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/91514c9af7e0f4c44029b51f05a01c6fe4c96e4c/src/Http/Routing/src/Matching/DfaMatcherBuilder.cs#L227-L244) is too abstracted from matching to be useful for understanding complex segment matching.

<a name="hostmatch"></a>

## <a name="host-matching-in-routes-with-requirehost"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-539">Corrispondenza host nelle route con RequireHost</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-539">Host matching in routes with RequireHost</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-540">`RequireHost` applica un vincolo alla route che richiede l'host specificato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-540">`RequireHost` applies a constraint to the route which requires the specified host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-541">Il parametro `RequireHost` o `[Host]` può essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-541">The `RequireHost` or `[Host]` parameter can be:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="49104-542">Host: `www.domain.com` (corrisponde `www.domain.com` con qualsiasi porta)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-542">Host: `www.domain.com` (matches `www.domain.com` with any port)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-543">Host con carattere jolly: `*.domain.com` (corrisponde a `www.domain.com`, `subdomain.domain.com`o `www.subdomain.domain.com` su qualsiasi porta)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-543">Host with wildcard: `*.domain.com` (matches `www.domain.com`, `subdomain.domain.com`, or `www.subdomain.domain.com` on any port)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-544">Port: `*:5000` (corrisponde alla porta 5000 con qualsiasi host)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-544">Port: `*:5000` (matches port 5000 with any host)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-545">Host e porta: `www.domain.com:5000`, `*.domain.com:5000` (corrisponde a host e porta)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-545">Host and port: `www.domain.com:5000`, `*.domain.com:5000` (matches host and port)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-546">È possibile specificare più parametri utilizzando `RequireHost` o `[Host]`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-546">Multiple parameters can be specified using `RequireHost` or `[Host]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-547">Il vincolo corrisponderà a host validi per uno qualsiasi dei parametri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-547">The constraint will match hosts valid for any of the parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-548">Ad esempio, `[Host("domain.com", "*.domain.com")]` corrisponderà `domain.com`, `www.domain.com`o `subdomain.domain.com`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-548">For example, `[Host("domain.com", "*.domain.com")]` will match `domain.com`, `www.domain.com`, or `subdomain.domain.com`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-549">Il codice seguente usa `RequireHost` per richiedere l'host specificato nella route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-549">The following code uses `RequireHost` to require the specified host on the route:</span></span>

```csharp
public void Configure(IApplicationBuilder app)
{
    app.UseRouting();

    app.UseEndpoints(endpoints =>
    {
        endpoints.MapGet("/", context => context.Response.WriteAsync("Hi Contoso!"))
            .RequireHost("contoso.com");
        endpoints.MapGet("/", context => context.Response.WriteAsync("Hi AdventureWorks!"))
            .RequireHost("adventure-works.com");
        endpoints.MapHealthChecks("/healthz").RequireHost("*:8080");
    });
}
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-550">Nel codice seguente viene utilizzato l'attributo `[Host]` per richiedere l'host specificato sul controller:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-550">The following code uses the `[Host]` attribute to require the specified host on the controller:</span></span>

```csharp
[Host("contoso.com", "adventure-works.com")]
public class HomeController : Controller
{
    private readonly ILogger<HomeController> _logger;

    public HomeController(ILogger<HomeController> logger)
    {
        _logger = logger;
    }

    public IActionResult Index()
    {
        return View();
    }

    [Host("example.com:8080")]
    public IActionResult Privacy()
    {
        return View();
    }

}
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-551">Quando l'attributo `[Host]` viene applicato sia al controller che al metodo di azione:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-551">When the `[Host]` attribute is applied to both the controller and action method:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="49104-552">Viene utilizzato l'attributo sull'azione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-552">The attribute on the action is used.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-553">L'attributo controller viene ignorato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-553">The controller attribute is ignored.</span></span>

::: moniker-end

::: moniker range="= aspnetcore-2.2"

<span data-ttu-id="49104-554">Il routing è responsabile del mapping degli URI di richiesta agli endpoint e dell'invio di richieste in ingresso a tali endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-554">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to endpoints and dispatching incoming requests to those endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-555">Le route sono definite nell'app e vengono configurate all'avvio dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-555">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-556">Una route può facoltativamente estrarre valori dall'URL contenuto nella richiesta e questi valori possono quindi essere usati per l'elaborazione della richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-556">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-557">Usando le informazioni sulla route dall'app, il routing è anche in grado di generare URL con mapping agli endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-557">Using route information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-558">Per usare gli scenari di routing più recenti in ASP.NET Core 2.2, specificare la [versione di compatibilità](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) nella registrazione dei servizi MVC in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-558">To use the latest routing scenarios in ASP.NET Core 2.2, specify the [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) to the MVC services registration in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddMvc()
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-559">L'opzione <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> determina se il routing deve usare internamente la logica basata sugli endpoint o la logica basata su <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> di ASP.NET Core 2.1 o versioni precedenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-559">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> option determines if routing should internally use endpoint-based logic or the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-560">Quando la versione di compatibilità è impostata su 2.2 o versioni successive, il valore predefinito è `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-560">When the compatibility version is set to 2.2 or later, the default value is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-561">Impostare il valore su `false` per usare la logica di routing precedente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-561">Set the value to `false` to use the prior routing logic:</span></span>

```csharp
// Use the routing logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier:
services.AddMvc(options => options.EnableEndpointRouting = false)
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-562">Per altre informazioni sul routing basato su <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, vedere la [versione per ASP.NET Core 2.1 di questo argomento](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-562">For more information on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, see the [ASP.NET Core 2.1 version of this topic](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-563">Questo documento descrive il routing di basso livello di ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-563">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-564">Per informazioni sul routing di ASP.NET Core MVC, vedere <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-564">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-565">Per informazioni sulle convenzioni di routing in Razor Pages, vedere <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-565">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-566">[Visualizzare o scaricare il codice di esempio](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([procedura per il download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-566">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-567">Nozioni fondamentali sul routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-567">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-568">La maggior parte delle app dovrebbe scegliere uno schema di routing semplice e descrittivo in modo che gli URL siano leggibili e significativi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-568">Most apps should choose a basic and descriptive routing scheme so that URLs are readable and meaningful.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-569">La route convenzionale predefinita `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-569">The default conventional route `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="49104-570">Supporta uno schema di routing semplice e descrittivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-570">Supports a basic and descriptive routing scheme.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-571">È un punto iniziale utile per le app basate su interfaccia utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-571">Is a useful starting point for UI-based apps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-572">Gli sviluppatori solitamente aggiungono ulteriori route brevi nelle aree a traffico elevato dell'app in situazioni specifiche (ad esempio, endpoint di blog e e-commerce) usando il [routing degli attributi](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) o route convenzionali dedicate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-572">Developers commonly add additional terse routes to high-traffic areas of an app in specialized situations (for example, blog and ecommerce endpoints) using [attribute routing](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) or dedicated conventional routes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-573">Le API Web devono usare il routing degli attributi per modellare le funzionalità dell'app come set di risorse in cui le operazioni sono rappresentate da verbi HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-573">Web APIs should use attribute routing to model the app's functionality as a set of resources where operations are represented by HTTP verbs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-574">Questo significa che molte operazioni (ad esempio, GET, POST) sulla stessa risorsa logica useranno lo stesso URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-574">This means that many operations (for example, GET, POST) on the same logical resource will use the same URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-575">Il routing degli attributi offre un livello di controllo necessario per progettare con attenzione il layout dell'endpoint pubblico di un'API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-575">Attribute routing provides a level of control that's needed to carefully design an API's public endpoint layout.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-576">Le app Razor Pages usano il routing convenzionale predefinito per servire le risorse denominate nella cartella *Pagine* dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-576">Razor Pages apps use default conventional routing to serve named resources in the *Pages* folder of an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-577">Sono disponibili convenzioni aggiuntive che consentono di personalizzare il comportamento di routing di Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-577">Additional conventions are available that allow you to customize Razor Pages routing behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-578">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:razor-pages/index> e <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-578">For more information, see <xref:razor-pages/index> and <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-579">Il supporto della generazione di URL consente di sviluppare l'app senza URL hardcoded per collegare l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-579">URL generation support allows the app to be developed without hard-coding URLs to link the app together.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-580">Il supporto consente di iniziare con una configurazione di routing di base e di modificare le route dopo aver determinato il layout delle risorse dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-580">This support allows for starting with a basic routing configuration and modifying the routes after the app's resource layout is determined.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-581">Il routing usa gli *endpoint* (`Endpoint`) per rappresentare gli endpoint logici in un'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-581">Routing uses *endpoints* (`Endpoint`) to represent logical endpoints in an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-582">Un endpoint definisce un delegato per l'elaborazione delle richieste e una raccolta di metadati arbitrari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-582">An endpoint defines a delegate to process requests and a collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-583">I metadati vengono usati per implementare gli elementi trasversali in base ai criteri e la configurazione associata a ogni endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-583">The metadata is used implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-584">Il sistema di routing ha le caratteristiche seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-584">The routing system has the following characteristics:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="49104-585">La sintassi del modello di route viene usata per definire le route con parametri di route in formato token.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-585">Route template syntax is used to define routes with tokenized route parameters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-586">La configurazione degli endpoint basata su convenzioni e attributi è consentita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-586">Conventional-style and attribute-style endpoint configuration is permitted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-587"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> consente di determinare se un parametro URL contiene un valore valido per il vincolo di un endpoint specifico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-587"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> is used to determine whether a URL parameter contains a valid value for a given endpoint constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-588">I modelli di app, ad esempio MVC o Razor Pages, registrano tutti i relativi endpoint, che hanno un'implementazione stimabile degli scenari di routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-588">App models, such as MVC/Razor Pages, register all of their endpoints, which have a predictable implementation of routing scenarios.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-589">L'implementazione del routing determina le decisioni relative al routing nel punto desiderato della pipeline del middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-589">The routing implementation makes routing decisions wherever desired in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-590">Il middleware successivo a un middleware di routing può esaminare il risultato della decisione dell'endpoint del middleware di routing per un URI di richiesta specifico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-590">Middleware that appears after a Routing Middleware can inspect the result of the Routing Middleware's endpoint decision for a given request URI.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-591">È possibile enumerare tutti gli endpoint nell'app in un punto qualsiasi della pipeline del middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-591">It's possible to enumerate all of the endpoints in the app anywhere in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-592">Un'app può usare il routing per generare URL, ad esempio per il reindirizzamento o i collegamenti, in base alle informazioni degli endpoint. In questo modo si evita di impostare gli URL come hardcoded ottimizzando la manutenibilità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-592">An app can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on endpoint information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-593">La generazione degli URL è basata sugli indirizzi, che supportano l'estensibilità arbitraria:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-593">URL generation is based on addresses, which support arbitrary extensibility:</span></span>
