<span data-ttu-id="49104-1067">Il routing specifica la classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> come implementazione standard di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1067">Routing provides the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class as the standard implementation of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1068"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> usa la sintassi del *modello di route* per definire i criteri in base ai quali confrontare il percorso URL quando si chiama <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1068"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> uses the *route template* syntax to define patterns to match against the URL path when <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> is called.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1069"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> usa lo stesso modello di route per generare un URL quando si chiama <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1069"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> uses the same route template to generate a URL when <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> is called.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1070">La maggior parte delle app crea le route chiamando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> o uno dei metodi di estensione simili definiti per <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1070">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1071">Tutti i metodi di estensione <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> creano un'istanza di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> e la aggiungono alla raccolta di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1071">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1072"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> non accetta alcun parametro del gestore di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1072"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1073"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> aggiunge solo le route che sono gestite da <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1073"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1074">Il gestore predefinito è `IRouter` e il gestore potrebbe non gestire la richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1074">The default handler is an `IRouter`, and the handler might not handle the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1075">Ad esempio, ASP.NET Core MVC viene in genere configurato come un gestore predefinito che gestisce solo le richieste che corrispondono a un'azione e un controller disponibili.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1075">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC is typically configured as a default handler that only handles requests that match an available controller and action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1076">Per altre informazioni sul routing in MVC, vedere <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1076">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1077">L'esempio di codice seguente si riferisce a una chiamata <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> usata da una tipica definizione di route di ASP.NET Core MVC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1077">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1078">Questo modello confronta un percorso URL ed estrae i valori di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1078">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1079">Ad esempio, il percorso `/Products/Details/17` genera i valori di route seguenti: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1079">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1080">I valori di route vengono determinati suddividendo il percorso URL in segmenti e confrontando ogni segmento con il nome del *parametro di route* nel modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1080">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1081">I parametri di route sono denominati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1081">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1082">Parametri definiti racchiudendo il nome del parametro tra parentesi graffe `{ ... }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1082">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1083">Il modello precedente può anche confrontare il percorso URL `/` e generare i valori `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1083">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1084">Ciò accade perché i parametri di route `{controller}` e `{action}` hanno valori predefiniti e il parametro di route `id` è facoltativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1084">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1085">Un segno di uguale (`=`) seguito da un valore dopo il nome del parametro di route definisce un valore predefinito per il parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1085">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1086">Un punto interrogativo (`?`) dopo il nome del parametro di route definisce un parametro facoltativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1086">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1087">I parametri di route con un valore predefinito producono *sempre* un valore di route quando la route corrisponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1087">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1088">I parametri facoltativi non producono alcun valore di route se non esiste un segmento di percorso URL corrispondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1088">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there was no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1089">Vedere la sezione [Riferimento per i modelli di route](#route-template-reference) per una descrizione completa degli scenari e della sintassi del modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1089">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1090">Nell'esempio seguente la definizione del parametro di route `{id:int}` definisce un [vincolo di route](#route-constraint-reference) per il parametro di route `id`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1090">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1091">Questo modello confronta un percorso URL come `/Products/Details/17`, ma non `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1091">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1092">I vincoli di route implementano <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> ed esaminano i valori di route per verificarli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1092">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1093">In questo esempio il valore di route `id` deve poter essere convertito in un numero intero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1093">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1094">Vedere [Riferimento per i vincoli di route](#route-constraint-reference) per una descrizione dei vincoli di route specificati dal framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1094">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1095">Altri overload di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accettano i valori per `constraints`, `dataTokens` e `defaults`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1095">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1096">L'uso tipico di questi parametri è passare un oggetto tipizzato in modo anonimo, in cui i nomi di proprietà di tipo anonimo corrispondono ai nomi dei parametri di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1096">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1097">Gli esempi <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> seguenti creano route equivalenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1097">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1098">La sintassi inline per definire i vincoli e i valori predefiniti può essere utile per le route semplici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1098">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1099">Esistono tuttavia scenari, come i token di dati, che non sono supportati dalla sintassi inline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1099">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1100">L'esempio seguente illustra alcuni scenari aggiuntivi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1100">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{*article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1101">Il modello precedente confronta un percorso URL come `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` ed estrae i valori `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1101">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1102">I valori di route predefiniti per `controller` e `action` vengono generati dalla route anche se sono non presenti parametri di route corrispondenti nel modello.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1102">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1103">I valori predefiniti possono essere specificati nel modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1103">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1104">Il parametro di route `article` è definito come *catch-all* in base alla presenza di un asterisco (`*`) prima del nome del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1104">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an asterisk (`*`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1105">I parametri di route catch-all acquisiscono il resto del percorso URL e possono anche corrispondere alla stringa vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1105">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1106">L'esempio seguente aggiunge i vincoli di route e i token di dati:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1106">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1107">Il modello precedente confronta un percorso URL come `/en-US/Products/5` ed estrae i valori `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` e i token di dati `{ locale = en-US }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1107">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![Token della finestra Variabili locali](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-1109">Generazione di URL della classe di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1109">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1110">La classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> è inoltre in grado di eseguire la generazione di URL combinando un set di valori di route con il relativo modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1110">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1111">Questo è logicamente il processo inverso di corrispondenza del percorso URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1111">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1112">Per comprendere meglio la generazione di URL, si pensi a quale URL si vuole generare e al modo in cui un modello di route deve corrispondere a tale URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1112">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1113">Quali valori devono essere prodotti?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1113">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1114">Questo equivale approssimativamente al funzionamento della generazione di URL nella classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1114">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1115">L'esempio seguente usa una route predefinita di ASP.NET Core MVC generale:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1115">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1116">Con i valori di route `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, viene generato l'URL `/Products/List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1116">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1117">I valori di route vengono sostituiti dai parametri di route corrispondenti per formare il percorso URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1117">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1118">Poiché `id` è un parametro di route facoltativo, l'URL è stato generato senza un valore per `id`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1118">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1119">Con i valori di route `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, viene generato l'URL `/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1119">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1120">Poiché i valori di route specificati corrispondono ai valori predefiniti, i segmenti corrispondenti ai valori predefiniti possono essere omessi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1120">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1121">Per entrambi gli URL generati viene eseguito il round trip con la definizione di route seguente (`/Home/Index` e `/`) e vengono prodotti gli stessi valori di route usati per generare l'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1121">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1122">Un'app che usa ASP.NET Core MVC deve usare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> per generare gli URL invece di eseguire la chiamata direttamente nel routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1122">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1123">Per altre informazioni sulla generazione di URL, vedere la sezione [Riferimento per la generazione di URL](#url-generation-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1123">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-1124">Usare il middleware di routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1124">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1125">Fare riferimento al [metapacchetto Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) nel file di progetto dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1125">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1126">Aggiungere il routing al contenitore del servizio in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1126">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1127">Le route devono essere configurate nel metodo `Startup.Configure`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1127">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1128">L'app di esempio usa le API seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1128">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="49104-1129"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Confronta solo le richieste HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1129"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1130">Nella tabella seguente sono elencate le risposte con gli URI specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1130">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1131">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1131">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1132">Risposta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1132">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1133">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1133">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1134">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1134">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1135">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1135">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1136">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1136">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1137">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1137">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1138">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1138">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1139">La richiesta non viene eseguita, nessuna corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1139">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1140">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1140">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1141">La richiesta non viene eseguita, corrispondenza solo con HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1141">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1142">La richiesta non viene eseguita, nessuna corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1142">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1143">Se si sta configurando una singola route, chiamare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passando un'istanza di `IRouter`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1143">If you're configuring a single route, call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passing in an `IRouter` instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1144">Non è necessario usare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1144">You won't need to use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1145">Il framework offre un set di metodi di estensione per la creazione di route (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1145">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1146">Alcuni dei metodi elencati, ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, richiedono <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1146">Some of listed methods, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, require a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1147"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> viene usato come *gestore di route* quando la route corrisponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1147">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> is used as the *route handler* when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1148">Altri metodi di questa famiglia consentono di configurare una pipeline middleware che verrà usata come gestore di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1148">Other methods in this family allow configuring a middleware pipeline for use as the route handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1149">Se il metodo `Map*` non accetta un gestore, ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, il metodo usa <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1149">If the `Map*` method doesn't accept a handler, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, it uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1150">I metodi `Map[Verb]` usano i vincoli per limitare la route al verbo HTTP nel nome del metodo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1150">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1151">Vedere ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1151">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-1152">Riferimento per il modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1152">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1153">I token all'interno di parentesi graffe (`{ ... }`) definiscono i *parametri di route* che vengono associati se esiste una corrispondenza per la route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1153">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1154">È possibile definire più parametri di route in un segmento di route, ma devono essere separati da un valore letterale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1154">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1155">Ad esempio, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` non è una route valida perché non è presente un valore letterale tra `{controller}` e `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1155">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1156">Questi parametri di route devono avere un nome e possono avere attributi aggiuntivi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1156">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1157">Il testo letterale diverso dai parametri di route, ad esempio `{id}`, e il separatore di percorso `/` devono corrispondere al testo nell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1157">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1158">La corrispondenza del testo non fa distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole e si basa sulla rappresentazione decodificata del percorso degli URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1158">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1159">Per verificare la corrispondenza di un delimitatore letterale dei parametri di route (`{` o `}`), eseguire l'escape del delimitatore ripetendo il carattere (`{{` o `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1159">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1160">I modelli di URL che tentano di acquisire un nome file con un'estensione facoltativa hanno considerazioni aggiuntive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1160">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1161">Considerare ad esempio il modello `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1161">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1162">Se esistono i valori per `filename` e `ext`, vengono popolati entrambi i valori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1162">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1163">Se esiste solo un valore per `filename` nell'URL, la route corrisponde perché il punto finale (`.`) è facoltativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1163">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1164">Gli URL seguenti corrispondono a questa route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1164">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1165">È possibile usare l'asterisco (`*`) come prefisso per un parametro di route da associare alla parte rimanente dell'URI,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1165">You can use the asterisk (`*`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1166">ovvero un parametro *catch-all*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1166">This is called a *catch-all* parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1167">Ad esempio, `blog/{*slug}` corrisponde a qualsiasi URI che inizia con `/blog` seguito da qualsiasi valore, che viene assegnato al valore di route `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1167">For example, `blog/{*slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1168">I parametri catch-all possono anche corrispondere alla stringa vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1168">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1169">Il parametro catch-all esegue l'escape dei caratteri appropriati, incluso il separatore di percorso (`/`), quando la route viene usata per generare un URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1169">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1170">Ad esempio, la route `foo/{*path}` con i valori di route `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1170">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1171">Si noti la barra di escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1171">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1172">I parametri di route possono avere *valori predefiniti*, definiti specificando il valore predefinito dopo il nome del parametro, separato da un segno di uguale (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1172">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1173">Ad esempio, `{controller=Home}` definisce `Home` come valore predefinito per `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1173">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1174">Il valore predefinito viene usato se nell'URL non è presente alcun valore per il parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1174">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1175">I parametri di route vengono resi facoltativi aggiungendo un punto interrogativo (`?`) alla fine del nome del parametro, come in `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1175">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1176">La differenza tra parametri facoltativi e parametri di route predefiniti è che un parametro di route con un valore predefinito produce sempre un valore, mentre un parametro facoltativo ha un valore solo se ne viene specificato uno dall'URL della richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1176">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1177">I parametri di route possono presentare dei vincoli che devono corrispondere al valore di route associato dall'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1177">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1178">Aggiungendo due punti (`:`) e il nome del vincolo dopo il nome del parametro di route, si specifica un *vincolo inline* per un parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1178">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1179">Se il vincolo richiede argomenti, vengono racchiusi tra parentesi (`(...)`) dopo il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1179">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1180">È possibile specificare più vincoli inline aggiungendo di nuovo i due punti (`:`) e il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1180">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1181">Il nome del vincolo e gli argomenti vengono passati al servizio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> per creare un'istanza di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> da usare nell'elaborazione dell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1181">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1182">Il modello di route `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifica ad esempio un vincolo `minlength` con l'argomento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1182">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1183">Per altre informazioni sui vincoli di route e per un elenco dei vincoli specificati dal framework, vedere la sezione [Riferimento per i vincoli di route](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1183">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1184">La tabella seguente illustra i modelli di route di esempio e il relativo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1184">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1185">Modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1185">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1186">URI corrispondente di esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1186">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1187">L'URI della richiesta&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1187">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1188">Verifica la corrispondenza solo del singolo percorso `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1188">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1189">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1189">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1190">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1190">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1191">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e all'azione `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1191">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1192">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e all'azione `Details` (`id` impostato su 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1192">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1193">Esegue il mapping al controller `Home` e al metodo `Index` (`id` viene ignorato).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1193">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1194">L'uso di un modello è in genere l'approccio più semplice al routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1194">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1195">I vincoli e le impostazioni predefinite possono essere specificati anche all'esterno del modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1195">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1196">Abilitare la [registrazione](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) per verificare in che modo le implementazioni del routing predefinite, ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, corrispondono alle richieste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1196">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-1197">Nomi riservati di routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1197">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1198">Le parole chiave seguenti sono nomi riservati e non possono essere usate come nomi o parametri di route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1198">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-1199">Riferimento per i vincoli di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1199">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1200">I vincoli di route vengono eseguiti quando si verifica una corrispondenza nell'URL in ingresso e il percorso URL viene suddiviso in valori di route in formato token.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1200">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1201">I vincoli di route in genere controllano il valore di route associato usando il modello di route e stabiliscono con una decisione Sì/No se il valore è accettabile o meno.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1201">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1202">Alcuni vincoli di route usano i dati all'esterno del valore di route per stabilire se la richiesta può essere instradata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1202">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1203">Ad esempio, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> può accettare o rifiutare una richiesta in base al relativo verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1203">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1204">I vincoli vengono usati nelle richieste del routing e nella generazione di collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1204">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1205">Non usare i vincoli per la **convalida dell'input**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1205">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1206">Se vengono usati vincoli per la **convalida dell'input**, un input non valido causa la visualizzazione di un errore di tipo *404 (Non trovato)* invece di un errore di tipo *400 - Richiesta non valida* con un messaggio di errore appropriato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1206">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1207">I vincoli di route vengono usati per evitare **ambiguità** tra route simili, non per convalidare gli input per una route specifica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1207">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1208">La tabella seguente illustra i vincoli di route di esempio e il relativo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1208">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1209">vincolo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1209">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1210">Esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1210">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1211">Esempi di corrispondenza</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1211">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1212">Note</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1212">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1213">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1213">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1214">Corrisponde a qualsiasi numero intero</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1214">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1215">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1215">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1216">Corrisponde a `true` o `false` (senza distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1216">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1217">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1217">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1218">Corrisponde a un valore `DateTime` valido (impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica, vedere avviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1218">Matches a valid `DateTime` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1219">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1219">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1220">Corrisponde a un valore `decimal` valido (impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica, vedere avviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1220">Matches a valid `decimal` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1221">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1221">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1222">Corrisponde a un valore `double` valido (impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica, vedere avviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1222">Matches a valid `double` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1223">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1223">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1224">Corrisponde a un valore `float` valido (impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica, vedere avviso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1224">Matches a valid `float` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1225">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1225">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1226">Corrisponde a un valore `Guid` valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1226">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1227">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1227">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1228">Corrisponde a un valore `long` valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1228">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1229">La stringa deve contenere almeno 4 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1229">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1230">La stringa non deve contenere più di 8 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1230">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1231">La stringa deve contenere esattamente 12 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1231">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1232">La stringa deve contenere almeno 8 e non più di 16 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1232">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1233">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1233">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1234">Il valore intero non deve essere superiore a 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1234">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1235">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18 ma non più di 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1235">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1236">La stringa deve essere costituita da uno o più caratteri alfabetici (`a`-`z`, senza distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1236">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1237">La stringa deve corrispondere all'espressione regolare (vedere i suggerimenti per la definizione di un'espressione regolare)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1237">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1238">Usato per imporre che un valore diverso da un parametro sia presente durante la generazione dell'URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1238">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1239">Più vincoli delimitati da punti possono essere applicati a un singolo parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1239">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1240">Ad esempio il vincolo seguente limita un parametro a un valore intero maggiore o uguale a 1:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1240">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1241">I vincoli di route che verificano l'URL e vengono convertiti in un tipo CLR, ad esempio `int` o `DateTime`, usano sempre le impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1241">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1242">presupponendo che l'URL sia non localizzabile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1242">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1243">I vincoli di route specificati dal framework non modificano i valori archiviati nei valori di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1243">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1244">Tutti i valori di route analizzati dall'URL vengono archiviati come stringhe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1244">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1245">Ad esempio, il vincolo `float` prova a convertire il valore di route in un valore float, ma il valore convertito viene usato solo per verificare che può essere convertito in un valore float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1245">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-1246">Espressioni regolari</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1246">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1247">Il framework di ASP.NET Core aggiunge `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` al costruttore di espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1247">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1248">Per una descrizione di questi membri, vedere <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1248">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1249">Le espressioni regolari usano delimitatori e token simili a quelli usati dal routing e dal linguaggio C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1249">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1250">Per i token di espressione è necessario aggiungere caratteri di escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1250">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1251">Per usare l'espressione regolare `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` nel routing, l'espressione deve includere i caratteri `\` (barra rovesciata singola) specificati nella stringa come caratteri `\\` (barra rovesciata doppia) nel file di origine C# per eseguire l'escape del carattere di escape della stringa `\`, a meno che non si usino [valori letterali di stringa verbatim](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1251">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1252">Per eseguire l'escape dii caratteri delimitatori dei parametri di routing (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), raddoppiare i caratteri nell'espressione (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1252">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1253">La tabella seguente mostra un'espressione regolare e la versione dopo l'escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1253">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1254">Espressione regolare</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1254">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1255">Espressione regolare con caratteri di escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1255">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1256">Le espressioni regolari usate nel routing spesso iniziano con l'accento circonflesso (`^`) e corrispondono alla posizione iniziale della stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1256">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1257">Le espressioni spesso terminano con il segno di dollaro (`$`) e corrispondono alla fine della stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1257">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1258">I caratteri `^` e `$` consentono di verificare che l'espressione regolare corrisponda all'intero valore del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1258">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1259">Senza i caratteri `^` e `$` l'espressione regolare corrisponde a qualsiasi sottostringa all'interno della stringa e spesso questo non è il risultato desiderato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1259">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1260">La tabella seguente include alcuni esempi e descrive perché si verifica o non si verifica la corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1260">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1261">Expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1261">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1262">Stringa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1262">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1263">Corrispondenza con</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1263">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1264">Commento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1264">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1265">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1265">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1266">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1266">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1267">Corrispondenze di sottostringhe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1267">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1268">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1268">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1269">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1269">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1270">Corrispondenze di sottostringhe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1270">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1271">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1271">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1272">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1272">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1273">Corrisponde all'espressione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1273">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1274">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1274">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1275">Yes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1275">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1276">Senza distinzione maiuscole/minuscole</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1276">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1277">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1277">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1278">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1278">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1279">Vedere `^` e `$` sopra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1279">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1280">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1280">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1281">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1281">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1282">Vedere `^` e `$` sopra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1282">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1283">Per altre informazioni sulla sintassi delle espressioni regolari, vedere [Espressioni regolari di .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1283">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1284">Per limitare un parametro a un set noto di valori possibili, usare un'espressione regolare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1284">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1285">Ad esempio, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` verifica la corrispondenza del valore di route `action` solo con `list`, `get` o `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1285">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1286">Se viene passata nel dizionario di vincoli, la stringa `^(list|get|create)$` è equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1286">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1287">Anche i vincoli passati nel dizionario di vincoli (non inline all'interno di un modello) che non corrispondono a uno dei vincoli noti vengono considerati espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1287">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-1288">Vincoli di route personalizzati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1288">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1289">Oltre ai vincoli di route predefiniti, è possibile creare vincoli di route personalizzati implementando l'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1289">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1290">L'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contiene un singolo metodo, `Match`, che restituisce `true` se il vincolo viene soddisfatto e `false` in caso contrario.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1290">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1291">Per usare un'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personalizzata, il tipo di vincolo di route deve essere registrato con la proprietà <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> dell'app nel contenitore di servizi dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1291">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1292"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> è un dizionario che esegue il mapping delle chiavi dei vincoli di route alle implementazioni di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> che convalidano tali vincoli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1292">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1293">La proprietà <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> di un'app può essere aggiornata in `Startup.ConfigureServices` come parte di una chiamata [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) o configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> direttamente con `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1293">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1294">Esempio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1294">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1295">Il vincolo può quindi essere applicato alle route nel modo consueto, usando il nome specificato al momento della registrazione del tipo di vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1295">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1296">Esempio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1296">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-1297">Riferimento per la generazione di URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1297">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1298">L'esempio seguente mostra come generare un collegamento a una route usando un dizionario di valori di route e un elemento <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1298">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1299">L'elemento <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generato alla fine dell'esempio precedente è `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1299">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1300">Il dizionario fornisce i valori di route `operation` e `id` del modello "Track Package Route", `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1300">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1301">Per informazioni dettagliate, vedere il codice di esempio nella sezione [Usare il middleware di routing](#use-routing-middleware) oppure l'[app di esempio](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1301">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1302">Il secondo parametro per il costruttore <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> è una raccolta di *valori di ambiente*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1302">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1303">I valori di ambiente sono utili poiché limitano il numero di valori che uno sviluppatore deve specificare all'interno del contesto di una richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1303">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1304">I valori di route correnti della richiesta corrente sono considerati valori di ambiente per la generazione del collegamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1304">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1305">Nell'azione `About` di un'app ASP.NET Core MVC di `HomeController`, non è necessario specificare il valore di route del controller per collegarsi all'azione `Index`. Viene usato il valore di ambiente `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1305">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1306">I valori di ambiente che non corrispondono a un parametro vengono ignorati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1306">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1307">I valori di ambiente vengono ignorati anche quando un valore specificato in modo esplicito esegue l'override del valore di ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1307">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1308">La corrispondenza si verifica da sinistra a destra nell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1308">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1309">I valori specificati in modo esplicito ma che non corrispondono a un segmento della route vengono aggiunti alla stringa di query.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1309">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1310">La tabella seguente illustra il risultato ottenuto quando si usa il modello di route `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1310">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1311">Valori di ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1311">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1312">Valori espliciti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1312">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1313">Risultato</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1313">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1314">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1314">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1315">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1315">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1316">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1316">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1317">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1317">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1318">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1318">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1319">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1319">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="49104-1320">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1320">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="49104-1321">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1321">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1322">Se una route ha un valore predefinito che non corrisponde a un parametro e tale valore viene specificato in modo esplicito, deve corrispondere al valore predefinito:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1322">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1323">La generazione dei collegamenti genera un collegamento per questa route quando vengono specificati i valori corrispondenti per `controller` e `action`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1323">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="49104-1324">Segmenti complessi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1324">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="49104-1325">I segmenti complessi (ad esempio, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`), vengono elaborati individuando corrispondenze per i valori letterali da destra a sinistra in modalità non-greedy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1325">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1326">Vedere [questo codice](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) per una spiegazione dettagliata di come vengono confrontati i segmenti complessi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1326">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49104-1327">L'[esempio di codice](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) non viene usato da ASP.NET Core, ma offre una spiegazione esauriente dei segmenti complessi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49104-1327">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
